-- =========================
-- RAYFIELD
-- =========================
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local player = Players.LocalPlayer
local playerScripts = player:WaitForChild("PlayerScripts")
local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")

local afkScripts = {}

local function scanAFKScripts()
    table.clear(afkScripts)

    for _, obj in ipairs(playerScripts:GetDescendants()) do
        if obj:IsA("LocalScript") then
            if string.find(string.lower(obj.Name), "afk") then
                table.insert(afkScripts, obj)
            end
        end
    end
end

local function disableAFK()
    scanAFKScripts()
    for _, scriptObj in ipairs(afkScripts) do
        if scriptObj and scriptObj.Parent then
            scriptObj.Enabled = false
        end
    end
end

local function enableAFK()
    for _, scriptObj in ipairs(afkScripts) do
        if scriptObj and scriptObj.Parent then
            scriptObj.Enabled = true
        end
    end
end

local Rayfield = loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://sirius.menu/rayfield"))()

local Window = Rayfield:CreateWindow({
   Name = "Index Hub - Replay System",
   LoadingTitle = "Carregando... (Index Hub)",
   LoadingSubtitle = "By (Namorada do Tevez)",
   Theme = "Amethyst",
   ToggleUIKeybind = "K",
   ConfigurationSaving = {
      Enabled = true,
      FileName = "Index Hub"
   }
})

-- SERVICES / PLAYER
-- =========================

local MovementsTable = {
   ["Replay 1"] = movements1,
   ["Replay 2"] = movements2,
   ["Replay 3"] = movements3,
   ["Replay 4"] = movements4
}

local currentMovements = nil

-- =========================
-- CONTROLE
-- =========================
local playing = false
local playConnection = nil
local currentIndex = 1

-- =========================
-- PLAY REPLAY
-- =========================
local function playMovements()
   if playing then return end
   if not currentMovements or #currentMovements == 0 then
      Rayfield:Notify({
         Title = "Erro",
         Content = "Nenhum replay selecionado!",
         Duration = 3
      })
      return
   end

   local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
   local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
   local rootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
   
   playing = true
   currentIndex = 1
   
   local startTime = tick()
   
   playConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
      local elapsed = tick() - startTime
      
      if currentIndex > #currentMovements then
         playConnection:Disconnect()
         playConnection = nil
         playing = false
         currentIndex = 1
         Rayfield:Notify({
            Title = "Replay",
            Content = "Replay finalizado!",
            Duration = 2
         })
         return
      end
      
      while currentIndex <= #currentMovements and currentMovements[currentIndex].time <= elapsed do
         local mov = currentMovements[currentIndex]
         local pos = Vector3.new(mov.position.x, mov.position.y, mov.position.z)
         local orient = Vector3.new(mov.orientation.x, mov.orientation.y, mov.orientation.z)
         
         rootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(pos) * CFrame.Angles(
            math.rad(orient.x),
            math.rad(orient.y),
            math.rad(orient.z)
         )
         
         -- Reproduzir estado do personagem
         if mov.state == "jumping" then
            humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
         elseif mov.state == "walking" or mov.state == "running" then
            humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running)
         elseif mov.state == "freefall" then
            humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Freefall)
         end
         
         currentIndex = currentIndex + 1
      end
   end)
end

-- =========================
-- STOP
-- =========================
local function stopReplay()
   playing = false
   currentIndex = 1
   if playConnection then
      playConnection:Disconnect()
      playConnection = nil
   end
   
   Rayfield:Notify({
      Title = "Replay",
      Content = "Replay parado",
      Duration = 2
   })
end

-- =========================
-- TABS
-- =========================
local MainTab = Window:CreateTab("Main", 7539983773)
local ReplayTab = Window:CreateTab("Replay", 4483362458)

-- =========================
-- MAIN TAB
-- =========================
MainTab:CreateButton({
   Name = "Test Button",
   Callback = function()
      Rayfield:Notify({
         Title = "Index Hub",
         Content = "Boto funcionando!",
         Duration = 3
      })
   end
})

local AntiAfk = MainTab:CreateToggle({
   Name = "Anti AFK",
   CurrentValue = false,
   Flag = "Anti AFK",
   Callback = function(Value)
       if Value then
           disableAFK()
       else
           enableAFK()
       end
   end,
})

-- =========================
-- REPLAY TAB
-- =========================
ReplayTab:CreateLabel("Sistema de Replay")

ReplayTab:CreateDropdown({
   Name = " Selecionar Replay",
   Options = {
      "Replay 1","Replay 2","Replay 3", "Replay 4"
   },
   CurrentOption = {},
   Callback = function(option)
      local selected = option[1]
      if not selected then return end

      currentMovements = MovementsTable[selected]

      Rayfield:Notify({
         Title = "Replay",
         Content = selected .. " selecionado",
         Duration = 2
      })
   end
})

ReplayTab:CreateButton({
   Name = " Play",
   Callback = playMovements
})

ReplayTab:CreateButton({
   Name = " Stop",
   Callback = stopReplay
})

print(" Index Hub - Replay System carregado com sucesso")
